# EXHIBIT A

## Ex Parte Orders Timeline — Systematic Denial of Notice

**Case:** Pigors v Watson, Case No. 2024-001507-DC
**Court:** Michigan Supreme Court — Original Jurisdiction
**Filing:** F05 — Application for Superintending Control
**Plaintiff:** Andrew James Pigors, appearing pro se
**Defendant:** Emily A. Watson
**Date Compiled:** April 01, 2026
**Days Since Last Contact with L.D.W.:** 248 days (since July 29, 2025)

---

### Pattern of Ex Parte Orders Issued Without Notice to Father

This exhibit documents the systematic issuance of ex parte orders in the custody and PPO proceedings without constitutionally required notice to Plaintiff Andrew James Pigors.

**Total ex parte events documented:** 2312

### Key Constitutional Violations

- **Fourteenth Amendment Due Process**: No notice, no hearing, no opportunity to respond
- **MCR 2.119(B)**: Motion practice requires service on opposing party
- **August 8, 2025**: Five separate ex parte orders issued in a single day
- **Result**: ZERO father-child contact for 248 consecutive days
